SELECT [t1].[EventDate], [t1].[Quota], [t1].[TicketCode], [t1].[TicketName], [t0].[Name] AS [CategoryName], [t1].[Price]
FROM (
    SELECT [t].[EventDate], [t].[Price], [t].[Quota], [t].[TicketCategoryId], [t].[TicketCode], [t].[TicketName]
    FROM [Tickets] AS [t]
    ORDER BY [t].[TicketCode]
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t1]
